Notice
No Legal responsibility is accepted for the publication of advertisements regarding 
change of name in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. Persons notifying the changes 
will remain solely responsible for the legal consequences and also for any other 
misrepresentation, etc.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE 	
 [Part VI—Sec. 4
public Notices
P. Rajendran, a male child born to Thiru K. Perumal, on 20th January 1981, residing at Kanchamalaipuravadai. Valathi, 
Siruthalaipoondi Post, Villupuram-604 201. has been living as a female. She has been granted an Identity Card No. 4539/09 
issued by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. by this I, may be treated as a Female 
and shall henceforth be known as P. RAFEENA
Villupuram,	
	
	
P. RAJENDRAN
10th February 2020.
	
S. Harini daughter of Thiru S. Sampath aged 31,  residing at New No. 9. Old No. 6. Bhujanga Rao Lane, Radha Nagar, 
Chromepet. Chennai-600 044. Wish to State that, I have Married Shri. V. Srivatsan son of Thiru R. Varadarajan, on 19th October 
2018, which was duly registered before Marriage Registrar, Chromepet, Chennai-600 044, On 26th October 2018, (No. 469/2018 
dated 26th October 2018).
At the time of Marriage with Shri. V. Srivatsan, he had one boy named S. Madhav, born on 19th September 2012. 
(Birth Certificate Register No. 2252/2012/56 dated 28th September 2012) for his (late) wife Mrs. M. Divya who expired 
on 2nd October 2012 (Death Certificate Register No. 260/2012/56 dated 15th October 2012)
By, Virtue of my Marriage with Shri V. Srivatsan I have become the Step Mother of S. Madhav.
The Public Notice is being issued by heartedly on my wiling without any prejudice/coercion.
Chennai,	
                                                                                                                                                       S. Harini
14th February 2020.	
(Step Mother).
